Motivation: 主动悬架系统对提升车辆舒适性、安全性和稳定性至关重要，但传统方法受限于固定的硬件设计和无法适应不确定动态工况的控制策略。数字孪生和深度强化学习为实时数据驱动优化提供了新机遇，但如何将这些技术集成到统一框架中仍是一个开放挑战。

Method: 提出基于数字孪生的控制协同设计框架，采用多代设计概念，将自动微分集成到深度强化学习中，联合优化物理悬架组件和控制策略。通过分位数学习进行模型更新以捕捉数据不确定性，解决部分可观测性问题，直接从可用传感器信息学习最优控制动作。

Result: 在两种不同驾驶场景（温和与激进）下实现悬架系统的个性化优化。优化后的系统实现了更平滑的轨迹，控制努力分别降低了约43%和52%，同时保持了乘坐舒适性和稳定性。

Conclusion: 开发了集成深度强化学习和不确定性感知模型更新的数字孪生协同设计框架，引入了自改进系统的多代设计策略，展示了针对不同驾驶员类型的主动悬架系统个性化优化。

Abstract: Active suspension systems are critical for enhancing vehicle comfort, safety, and stability, yet their performance is often limited by fixed hardware designs and control strategies that cannot adapt to uncertain and dynamic operating conditions. Recent advances in digital twins (DTs) and deep reinforcement learning (DRL) offer new opportunities for real-time, data-driven optimization across a vehicle's lifecycle. However, integrating these technologies into a unified framework remains an open challenge. This work presents a DT-based control co-design (CCD) framework for full-vehicle active suspensions using multi-generation design concepts. By integrating automatic differentiation into DRL, we jointly optimize physical suspension components and control policies under varying driver behaviors and environmental uncertainties. DRL also addresses the challenge of partial observability, where only limited states can be sensed and fed back to the controller, by learning optimal control actions directly from available sensor information. The framework incorporates model updating with quantile learning to capture data uncertainty, enabling real-time decision-making and adaptive learning from digital-physical interactions. The approach demonstrates personalized optimization of suspension systems under two distinct driving settings (mild and aggressive). Results show that the optimized systems achieve smoother trajectories and reduce control efforts by approximately 43% and 52% for mild and aggressive, respectively, while maintaining ride comfort and stability. Contributions include: developing a DT-enabled CCD framework integrating DRL and uncertainty-aware model updating for full-vehicle active suspensions, introducing a multi-generation design strategy for self-improving systems, and demonstrating personalized optimization of active suspension systems for distinct driver types.

中文标题: 基于数字孪生和深度强化学习的整车主动悬架协同设计

中文摘要: 主动悬架系统对提升车辆舒适性、安全性和稳定性至关重要，但其性能往往受限于固定的硬件设计和无法适应不确定动态工况的控制策略。数字孪生和深度强化学习的最新进展为车辆全生命周期的实时数据驱动优化提供了新机遇。然而，将这些技术集成到统一框架中仍是一个开放挑战。本研究提出了一种基于数字孪生的整车主动悬架控制协同设计框架，采用多代设计概念。通过将自动微分集成到深度强化学习中，我们在变化的驾驶员行为和环境不确定性下联合优化物理悬架组件和控制策略。深度强化学习还通过直接从可用传感器信息学习最优控制动作，解决了部分可观测性的挑战，即只有有限状态可以被感知并反馈给控制器。该框架结合了分位数学习的模型更新以捕捉数据不确定性，实现了实时决策和数字-物理交互的自适应学习。该方法展示了在两种不同驾驶场景（温和与激进）下悬架系统的个性化优化。结果表明，优化后的系统实现了更平滑的轨迹，控制努力分别降低了约43%和52%，同时保持了乘坐舒适性和稳定性。贡献包括：开发了集成深度强化学习和不确定性感知模型更新的数字孪生协同设计框架用于整车主动悬架；引入了自改进系统的多代设计策略；展示了针对不同驾驶员类型的主动悬架系统个性化优化。

</details>


### [106] [Driving is a Game: Combining Planning and Prediction with Bayesian Iterative Best Response](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03936)
*Aron Distelzweig,Yiwei Wang,Faris Janjoš,Marcel Hallgarten,Mihai Dobre,Alexander Langmann,Joschka Boedecker,Johannes Betz*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: BIBeR框架将最先进的运动预测器集成到博弈论迭代最优响应循环中，实现自动驾驶车辆与其他交通参与者的双向交互适应，在交互场景中显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前自动驾驶规划系统在常规场景表现良好，但在密集城市交通中面临挑战，特别是需要预测和影响其他交通参与者的车道变更和并线场景。现有方法要么将预测与规划简单分离，要么采用单向的端到端模型，缺乏在不确定性下联合建模预测和规划的能力。博弈论方法提供了原则性解决方案但应用有限。

Method: 提出贝叶斯迭代最优响应（BIBeR）框架：1）将最先进的运动预测器集成到迭代最优响应（IBR）循环中，反复优化自车和周围交通参与者的策略；2）通过重复最优响应过程近似纳什均衡，实现双向适应；3）引入贝叶斯置信度估计量化预测可靠性，动态调节策略更新强度。

Result: 在高度交互的interPlan车道变更场景中，BIBeR比最先进的规划器实现了11%的改进。在标准nuPlan基准测试中也优于现有方法。框架与现代预测器和规划器兼容，结合了结构化规划的透明性和学习模型的灵活性。

Conclusion: BIBeR成功地将博弈论规划与现代运动预测器相结合，为自动驾驶在密集交互场景中的决策提供了有效的解决方案。通过迭代最优响应和贝叶斯置信度调节，实现了预测与规划的深度集成，显著提升了在复杂交通环境中的性能。

Abstract: Autonomous driving planning systems perform nearly perfectly in routine scenarios using lightweight, rule-based methods but still struggle in dense urban traffic, where lane changes and merges require anticipating and influencing other agents. Modern motion predictors offer highly accurate forecasts, yet their integration into planning is mostly rudimental: discarding unsafe plans. Similarly, end-to-end models offer a one-way integration that avoids the challenges of joint prediction and planning modeling under uncertainty. In contrast, game-theoretic formulations offer a principled alternative but have seen limited adoption in autonomous driving. We present Bayesian Iterative Best Response (BIBeR), a framework that unifies motion prediction and game-theoretic planning into a single interaction-aware process. BIBeR is the first to integrate a state-of-the-art predictor into an Iterative Best Response (IBR) loop, repeatedly refining the strategies of the ego vehicle and surrounding agents. This repeated best-response process approximates a Nash equilibrium, enabling bidirectional adaptation where the ego both reacts to and shapes the behavior of others. In addition, our proposed Bayesian confidence estimation quantifies prediction reliability and modulates update strength, more conservative under low confidence and more decisive under high confidence. BIBeR is compatible with modern predictors and planners, combining the transparency of structured planning with the flexibility of learned models. Experiments show that BIBeR achieves an 11% improvement over state-of-the-art planners on highly interactive interPlan lane-change scenarios, while also outperforming existing approaches on standard nuPlan benchmarks.

中文标题: 驾驶是一场博弈：将规划与预测结合贝叶斯迭代最优响应

中文摘要: 自动驾驶规划系统在常规场景中使用轻量级、基于规则的方法表现近乎完美，但在密集的城市交通中仍然面临挑战，其中车道变更和并线需要预测和影响其他交通参与者。现代运动预测器提供高度准确的预测，但它们与规划的集成大多停留在初级阶段：仅丢弃不安全计划。类似地，端到端模型提供单向集成，避免了在不确定性下联合预测和规划建模的挑战。相比之下，博弈论公式提供了原则性的替代方案，但在自动驾驶中的应用有限。我们提出了贝叶斯迭代最优响应（BIBeR），这是一个将运动预测和博弈论规划统一为单一交互感知过程的框架。BIBeR首次将最先进的预测器集成到迭代最优响应（IBR）循环中，反复优化自车和周围交通参与者的策略。这种重复的最优响应过程近似于纳什均衡，实现了双向适应，其中自车既对其他交通参与者的行为做出反应，又塑造他们的行为。此外，我们提出的贝叶斯置信度估计量化了预测可靠性并调节更新强度，在低置信度下更保守，在高置信度下更果断。BIBeR与现代预测器和规划器兼容，结合了结构化规划的透明性和学习模型的灵活性。实验表明，在高度交互的interPlan车道变更场景中，BIBeR比最先进的规划器实现了11%的改进，同时在标准nuPlan基准测试中也优于现有方法。

</details>


### [107] [MDE-AgriVLN: Agricultural Vision-and-Language Navigation with Monocular Depth Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03958)
*Xiaobei Zhao,Xingqi Lyu,Xiang Li*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: MDE-AgriVLN方法通过单目深度估计增强农业视觉语言导航，在A2A基准上成功率达到0.32，导航误差降至4.08m，实现了农业VLN领域的最先进性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 农业机器人通常只配备单目摄像头，导致空间感知能力有限，而现有的AgriVLN方法和A2A基准虽然将视觉语言导航扩展到农业领域，但缺乏深度感知能力，限制了导航性能。

Method: 提出MDE-AgriVLN方法，包含MDE模块从RGB图像生成深度特征，辅助决策模块进行推理。该方法通过单目深度估计增强空间感知能力，提升农业机器人在自然语言指令下的导航性能。

Result: 在A2A基准测试中，MDE-AgriVLN将成功率从0.23提升到0.32，导航误差从4.43m降低到4.08m，在农业VLN领域实现了最先进的性能。

Conclusion: 单目深度估计能有效增强农业机器人的空间感知能力，显著提升视觉语言导航性能，为农业机器人自主导航提供了新的解决方案。

Abstract: Agricultural robots are serving as powerful assistants across a wide range of agricultural tasks, nevertheless, still heavily relying on manual operations or railway systems for movement. The AgriVLN method and the A2A benchmark pioneeringly extend Vision-and-Language Navigation (VLN) to the agricultural domain, enabling a robot to navigate to a target position following a natural language instruction. Unlike human binocular vision, most agricultural robots are only given a single camera for monocular vision, which results in limited spatial perception. To bridge this gap, we present the method of Agricultural Vision-and-Language Navigation with Monocular Depth Estimation (MDE-AgriVLN), in which we propose the MDE module generating depth features from RGB images, to assist the decision-maker on reasoning. When evaluated on the A2A benchmark, our MDE-AgriVLN method successfully increases Success Rate from 0.23 to 0.32 and decreases Navigation Error from 4.43m to 4.08m, demonstrating the state-of-the-art performance in the agricultural VLN domain. Code: https://github.com/AlexTraveling/MDE-AgriVLN.

中文标题: MDE-AgriVLN：基于单目深度估计的农业视觉语言导航

中文摘要: 农业机器人作为强大的助手服务于广泛的农业任务，但仍然严重依赖手动操作或轨道系统进行移动。AgriVLN方法和A2A基准开创性地将视觉语言导航扩展到农业领域，使机器人能够按照自然语言指令导航到目标位置。与人类双目视觉不同，大多数农业机器人只配备单目摄像头，导致空间感知能力有限。为了弥补这一差距，我们提出了基于单目深度估计的农业视觉语言导航方法，其中我们提出了MDE模块从RGB图像生成深度特征，以辅助决策模块进行推理。在A2A基准测试中，我们的MDE-AgriVLN方法成功将成功率从0.23提高到0.32，将导航误差从4.43m降低到4.08m，在农业VLN领域展示了最先进的性能。

### [108] [Artificial Microsaccade Compensation: Stable Vision for an Ornithopter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03995)
*Levi Burner,Guido de Croon,Yiannis Aloimonos*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出了一种受生物微扫视启发的视频稳定方法，专门解决扑翼无人机因高频振动（12-20Hz）导致的视频抖动问题，通过SO(3)空间优化实现实时无失真稳定，性能优于商业软件Adobe Premiere Pro的变形稳定器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受生物微扫视现象的启发，解决无尾扑翼无人机因高频振动（12-20Hz）而无法使用相机传感的问题。传统方法难以处理这种特定频率的抖动，需要一种能实时稳定视频且无失真的解决方案。

Method: 开发了"人工微扫视补偿"方法，通过优化SO(3)空间中的3D旋转表示来最小化图像强度变化。该方法支持实时计算，产生适合人眼观看的无失真稳定视频。当适应固定观看方向时（偶尔进行扫视），能显著减少帧间运动，并受益于高效的递归更新机制。

Result: 与广泛认为最佳的商业视频稳定软件Adobe Premiere Pro的变形稳定器相比，该方法实现了更高质量的结果，同时能够实时运行。成功稳定了扑翼无人机在12-20Hz振动下拍摄的视频。

Conclusion: 受生物微扫视启发的视频稳定方法有效解决了扑翼无人机的高频振动问题，实现了实时、高质量、无失真的视频稳定，性能优于现有商业解决方案。

Abstract: Animals with foveated vision, including humans, experience microsaccades, small, rapid eye movements that they are not aware of. Inspired by this phenomenon, we develop a method for "Artificial Microsaccade Compensation". It can stabilize video captured by a tailless ornithopter that has resisted attempts to use camera-based sensing because it shakes at 12-20 Hz. Our approach minimizes changes in image intensity by optimizing over 3D rotation represented in SO(3). This results in a stabilized video, computed in real time, suitable for human viewing, and free from distortion. When adapted to hold a fixed viewing orientation, up to occasional saccades, it can dramatically reduce inter-frame motion while also benefiting from an efficient recursive update. When compared to Adobe Premier Pro's warp stabilizer, which is widely regarded as the best commercial video stabilization software available, our method achieves higher quality results while also running in real time.

中文标题: 人工微扫视补偿：为扑翼无人机提供稳定视觉

中文摘要: 具有中央凹视觉的动物（包括人类）会经历微扫视，即小而快速的眼球运动，它们自己并未意识到。受此现象启发，我们开发了一种"人工微扫视补偿"方法。它可以稳定由无尾扑翼无人机拍摄的视频，这种无人机因以12-20 Hz的频率振动而一直难以使用基于相机的传感。我们的方法通过优化SO(3)中表示的3D旋转来最小化图像强度的变化。这产生了一个稳定视频，实时计算，适合人眼观看，且无失真。当适应于保持固定观看方向（偶尔进行扫视）时，它能显著减少帧间运动，同时受益于高效的递归更新。与广泛认为最佳商业视频稳定软件Adobe Premiere Pro的变形稳定器相比，我们的方法实现了更高质量的结果，同时也能实时运行。

### [109] [Head, posture, and full-body gestures in interactive communication](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03636)
*Ľuboš Hládek,Bernhard U. Seeber*

Main category: cs.HC

TL;DR: 研究发现背景噪音增加时，说话者和听者都会增加手部手势复杂性，头部上下运动更明显，但听者头部运动相对减少；言语-手势同步性基本不受噪音影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是探索在声学不利条件下（如背景噪音）面对面交流时，全身运动如何适应沟通需求。先前研究主要关注头部或手部运动的单一模态，而本研究旨在全面考察全身运动在困难沟通环境中的作用。

Method: 采用虚拟声学环境中的自由双人对话实验，参与者为8名正常听力者。开发了新的对话动作标签系统来描述全身运动，分析不同类型运动的频率。同时评估手语同步性来测量手势质量，检验噪音水平对同步性的影响。

Result: 背景噪音增加导致：1）说话和听的过程中手部手势复杂性增加；2）更明显的上下头部运动；3）听的过程中头部运动相对说话减少。言语-手势同步性和峰值速度不受噪音影响，手势质量仅适度变化。

Conclusion: 研究支持噪音环境下手势频率增加的发现，但言语-手势同步性变化有限。这表明全身运动在困难沟通环境中表现出多模态适应，但同步性机制相对稳定。研究为理解多模态沟通适应提供了新视角。

Abstract: When face-to-face communication becomes effortful due to background noise or interfering talkers, the role of visual cues becomes increasingly important for communication success. While previous research has selectively examined head or hand movements, here we explore movements of the whole body in acoustically adverse conditions. We hypothesized that increasing background noise in conversations would lead to increased gesture frequency in hand, head, trunk, and leg movements typical of conversation. Increased use of hand movements should support the speaker's role, while increased head and trunk movements may help the listener. We conducted a free dyadic conversation experiment with normal-hearing participants (n=8) in a virtual acoustic environment. Conversational movements were described with a newly developed labeling system for typical conversational actions, and the frequency of individual types was analyzed. In addition, we analyzed gesture quality by assessing hand-speech synchrony, with the hypothesis that higher levels of background noise would lead to a loss of synchrony according to an interactive coupling model. Higher noise levels led to increased hand-gesture complexity during speaking and listening, more pronounced up-down head movements, and contrary to expectations, head movements during listening generally decreased relative to speaking. Synchrony and peak velocity were unaffected by noise, while gesture quality scaled only modestly. The results support previous findings regarding gesturing frequency, but we found only limited evidence for changes in speech-gesture synchrony. This work reveals communication patterns of the whole body and illustrates multimodal adaptation to communication demands.

中文标题: 交互沟通中的头部、姿势和全身手势

中文摘要: 当面对面的交流因背景噪音或干扰性谈话者而变得费力时，视觉线索的作用对沟通成功变得越来越重要。虽然先前的研究选择性地考察了头部或手部运动，但本文探讨了在声学不利条件下全身的运动。我们假设对话中增加的背景噪音会导致手、头、躯干和腿部运动中典型对话手势频率的增加。手部运动的增加应支持说话者的角色，而头部和躯干运动的增加可能有助于听者。我们在虚拟声学环境中进行了一项自由双人对话实验，参与者为正常听力者（n=8）。对话运动使用新开发的典型对话动作标签系统进行描述，并分析了个别类型的频率。此外，我们通过评估手语同步性来分析手势质量，假设更高水平的背景噪音会导致根据交互耦合模型失去同步性。更高的噪音水平导致说话和听的过程中手部手势复杂性增加，更明显的上下头部运动，但出乎意料的是，听的过程中头部运动相对于说话普遍减少。同步性和峰值速度不受噪音影响，而手势质量仅适度变化。结果支持先前关于手势频率的发现，但我们只发现了言语-手势同步性变化的有限证据。这项工作揭示了全身的沟通模式，并说明了多模态对沟通需求的适应。

</details>


### [110] [Smartphone Vibrometric Force Estimation for Grip Related Strength Measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03186)
*Colin Barry,Edward Jay Wang*

Main category: cs.HC

TL;DR: 研究人员开发了一种仅使用智能手机内置振动电机和IMU传感器来估计握力相关力量的新方法，通过手指力调制振动信号实现力估计，在Google Pixel 4上验证显示绝对力误差1.88磅，相对误差10.1%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手握力是重要的临床健康指标，但传统测量设备不便携且成本高。本研究旨在探索仅使用智能手机内置传感器进行握力相关力量测量的可行性，为大规模、低负担的健康监测提供新方法。

Method: 利用智能手机振动电机产生振动，通过手指施加的力调制高频加速度计和陀螺仪信号（振动测量力估计）。使用Google Pixel 4收集同步IMU数据和真实力测量数据，训练脊回归模型进行绝对和相对力预测，采用15折留一验证方法。

Result: 绝对力估计的平均绝对误差为1.88磅，相对力估计的平均误差为10.1%。虽然测量的是捏力而非标准全手握力，但证明了仅使用智能手机传感器进行力量评估的技术可行性。

Conclusion: 该方法展示了仅使用智能手机内置传感器进行握力相关力量测量的可行性，为大规模、低成本的健康监测提供了潜在解决方案。一旦为不同手机型号完成分析，可能实现广泛的功能健康测量应用。

Abstract: Hand grip strength is a widely used clinical biomarker linked to mobility, frailty, surgical outcomes, and overall health. This work explores a novel, phone only approach for estimating grip related force using a smartphone's built in vibration motor and inertial measurement unit. When the phone vibrates, applied finger force modulates the amplitude of high frequency accelerometer and gyroscope signals through Vibrometric Force Estimation. We profiled a Google Pixel 4 using synchronized IMU data and ground truth force measurements across varied force trajectories, then trained ridge regression models for both absolute and relative force prediction. In 15 fold hold one out validation, absolute force estimation achieved a mean absolute error of 1.88 lbs, while relative force estimation achieved a mean error of 10.1%. Although the method captures pinch type force rather than standardized full hand HGS, the results demonstrate the feasibility of smartphone based strength assessment using only on device sensors. This approach may enable large scale, low burden functional health measurements once profiling is completed for major smartphone models.

中文标题: 智能手机振动测量力估计用于握力相关强度测量

中文摘要: 手握力是一种广泛使用的临床生物标志物，与活动能力、虚弱程度、手术结果和整体健康状况相关。本研究探索了一种新颖的、仅使用手机的方法来估计握力相关力量，利用智能手机内置的振动电机和惯性测量单元。当手机振动时，施加的手指力通过振动测量力估计来调制高频加速度计和陀螺仪信号的振幅。我们使用同步的IMU数据和真实力测量对Google Pixel 4进行了分析，涵盖了不同的力轨迹，然后训练了脊回归模型用于绝对和相对力预测。在15折留一验证中，绝对力估计实现了1.88磅的平均绝对误差，而相对力估计实现了10.1%的平均误差。虽然该方法捕捉的是捏力类型的力量而非标准化的全手握力，但结果证明了仅使用设备传感器进行基于智能手机的强度评估的可行性。一旦为主要的智能手机型号完成分析，这种方法可能实现大规模、低负担的功能健康测量。

</details>


### [111] [DAWZY: A New Addition to AI powered "Human in the Loop" Music Co-creation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03289)
*Aaron C Elkins,Sanchit Singh,Adrian Kieback,Sawyer Blankenship,Uyiosa Philip Amadasun,Aman Chadha*

Main category: cs.HC

TL;DR: DAWZY是一个开源AI助手，通过自然语言（文本/语音/哼唱）将用户意图转换为REAPER中的可逆操作，减少用户学习复杂DAW界面的时间，保持DAW作为创意中心，同时支持实时状态查询、参数调整和AI节拍生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统数字音频工作站（DAW）提供精细控制，但将高层意图（如"温暖人声"）映射到低层编辑会打断创作流程。现有AI音乐生成器通常是一次性的，限制了迭代开发和人类贡献的机会。需要一种工具能在保持DAW作为创意中心的同时，通过自然语言接口简化复杂操作。

Method: DAWZY采用基于LLM的代码生成方法，将自然语言请求转换为REAPER中的可逆操作。它使用三个模型上下文协议工具：实时状态查询、参数调整和AI节拍生成。系统通过突变前刷新状态保持基础，使用原子脚本和撤销功能确保安全性和可逆性，提供最小化GUI和语音优先界面。

Result: 在评估中，DAWZY在常见制作任务上表现可靠，在可用性、控制性、学习性、协作性和愉悦性方面获得用户积极评价。系统显著减少了用户熟悉大型界面的时间，用聊天框替代了数百个按钮和下拉菜单。

Conclusion: DAWZY成功地将AI辅助引入"人在回路"音乐共创，通过自然语言接口在保持DAW作为创意中心的同时简化了复杂操作，为迭代开发和人类贡献提供了新机会，是AI赋能音乐创作的有前景方向。

Abstract: Digital Audio Workstations (DAWs) offer fine control, but mapping high-level intent (e.g., "warm the vocals") to low-level edits breaks creative flow. Existing artificial intelligence (AI) music generators are typically one-shot, limiting opportunities for iterative development and human contribution. We present DAWZY, an open-source assistant that turns natural-language (text/voice/hum) requests into reversible actions in REAPER. DAWZY keeps the DAW as the creative hub with a minimal GUI and voice-first interface. DAWZY uses LLM-based code generation as a novel way to significantly reduce the time users spend familiarizing themselves with large interfaces, replacing hundreds of buttons and drop-downs with a chat box. DAWZY also uses three Model Context Protocol tools for live state queries, parameter adjustment, and AI beat generation. It maintains grounding by refreshing state before mutation and ensures safety and reversibility with atomic scripts and undo. In evaluations, DAWZY performed reliably on common production tasks and was rated positively by users across Usability, Control, Learning, Collaboration, and Enjoyment.

中文标题: DAWZY：AI驱动的"人在回路"音乐共创新成员

中文摘要: 数字音频工作站（DAW）提供精细控制，但将高层意图（如"温暖人声"）映射到低层编辑会打断创作流程。现有的人工智能（AI）音乐生成器通常是一次性的，限制了迭代开发和人类贡献的机会。我们提出了DAWZY，这是一个开源助手，可将自然语言（文本/语音/哼唱）请求转换为REAPER中的可逆操作。DAWZY保持DAW作为创意中心，提供最小化GUI和语音优先界面。DAWZY使用基于LLM的代码生成作为新方法，显著减少用户熟悉大型界面的时间，用聊天框替代数百个按钮和下拉菜单。DAWZY还使用三个模型上下文协议工具进行实时状态查询、参数调整和AI节拍生成。它通过突变前刷新状态保持基础，并使用原子脚本和撤销功能确保安全性和可逆性。在评估中，DAWZY在常见制作任务上表现可靠，在可用性、控制性、学习性、协作性和愉悦性方面获得用户积极评价。

### [112] [Teacher, But Also Student: Challenges and Tech Needs of Adult Braille Learners with Sight](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03398)
*Quan Zhou,Cameron Cassidy,Alyson Yin,Stacy Branham*

Main category: cs.HC

TL;DR: 该研究关注视力正常的成人盲文教师的学习挑战，发现他们缺乏持续接触、练习时间有限，需要更高效有趣的学习工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 盲文读写能力对盲人至关重要，但识字率持续下降。虽然盲文教师在盲人青少年读写发展中起核心作用，但现有研究几乎完全集中在盲人青少年学生身上，对视力正常的成人教师如何学习盲文了解甚少。

Method: 研究采访了14名教育工作者（13名认证视觉障碍学生教师和1名辅助教育工作者），他们都是在成年后学习盲文的，通过定性访谈了解他们的学习经历和挑战。

Result: 研究发现成人盲文教师面临三大挑战：1）缺乏持续的盲文接触来巩固知识和技能；2）由于成年后的诸多责任，练习时间有限；3）因此寻求既有趣又高效的学习工具。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了一个被忽视的盲文学习者群体（视力正常的成人教师）的需求，并指出了促进盲文读写能力的新设计机会，强调需要开发更适合成人学习特点的盲文学习工具和方法。

Abstract: Braille literacy is critical for blind individuals' independence and quality of life, yet literacy rates continue to decline. Though braille instructors in integrated K-12 classrooms play a central role in literacy development in blind youth, prior research on braille learning almost exclusively focuses on blind adolescent students. As a result, we still know little about how sighted adult teachers learn braille. To address this, we interviewed 14 educators, including 13 certificated Teachers of Students with Visual Impairments (TVIs) and 1 paraeducator, who learned braille as adults. We found that they: (1) lack consistent braille exposure to reinforce knowledge and skill; (2) have limited time to practice due to myriad responsibilities of adulthood; and thus, (3) seek learning tools that are engaging and efficient. Our research draws attention to the needs of a group of braille learners who have been overlooked and identifies new design opportunities to facilitate braille literacy.

### [113] [Why Some Seek AI, Others Seek Therapists: Mental Health in the Age of Generative AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03406)
*Junsang Park,Sarah Brown,Sharon Lynn Chu*

Main category: cs.HC

TL;DR: 研究发现治疗师在情感支持和个性化方面更受重视，而AI在可及性和成本方面有优势。情感效益和个性化是采用的关键因素，不同群体对AI的态度不同（学生视为补充，成人视为替代），隐私和可靠性担忧限制了AI使用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着生成式AI进入心理健康领域，需要了解人们如何在AI工具和人类治疗师之间做出选择，以及影响这些选择的信念因素。研究旨在探索不同群体对这两种心理健康服务模式的偏好和采用意向。

Method: 基于健康信念模型（HBM），在两个群体中进行研究：大学样本（N=1,155）和全国代表性成人样本（N=651）。使用重复测量方差分析和LASSO回归分析数据，考察信念因素对使用GAI和治疗师意向的预测作用。

Result: 治疗师在情感、关系和个性化方面始终更受重视；GAI在可及性和可负担性方面更受青睐。情感效益和个性化是采用的关键决定因素。学生将GAI视为补充，而全国成人样本将其视为替代品。隐私和可靠性担忧限制了GAI的使用。

Conclusion: 研究扩展了健康信念模型在多模态情境下的应用，强调了设计可信赖、情感共鸣的数字心理健康工具的重要性。不同群体对AI的态度差异表明需要针对性地设计心理健康服务。

Abstract: As generative artificial intelligence (GAI) enters the mental health landscape, questions arise about how individuals weigh AI tools against human therapists. Drawing on the Health Belief Model (HBM), this study examined belief-based predictors of intention to use GAI and therapists across two populations: a university sample (N = 1,155) and a nationally representative adult sample (N = 651). Using repeated-measures ANOVA and LASSO regression, we found that therapists were consistently valued for emotional, relational, and personalization benefits, while GAI was favored for accessibility and affordability. Yet structural advantages alone did not predict adoption; emotional benefit and personalization emerged as decisive factors. Adoption patterns diverged across groups: students treated GAI as a complement, whereas national adults approached it as a substitute. Concerns about privacy and reliability constrained GAI use in both groups. These findings extend HBM to multi-modality contexts and highlight design implications for trustworthy, emotionally resonant digital mental health tools.

中文标题: 为什么有人寻求AI，有人寻求治疗师：生成式AI时代的心理健康

中文摘要: 随着生成式人工智能（GAI）进入心理健康领域，人们开始思考个体如何在AI工具和人类治疗师之间进行权衡。本研究基于健康信念模型（HBM），考察了两个群体中基于信念的预测因素对使用GAI和治疗师意向的影响：大学样本（N = 1,155）和全国代表性成人样本（N = 651）。通过重复测量方差分析和LASSO回归，我们发现治疗师在情感、关系和个性化方面始终受到重视，而GAI则在可及性和可负担性方面更受青睐。然而，结构性优势本身并不能预测采用情况；情感效益和个性化成为决定性因素。不同群体的采用模式存在差异：学生将GAI视为补充，而全国成人样本则将其视为替代品。对隐私和可靠性的担忧限制了两个群体对GAI的使用。这些发现将HBM扩展到多模态情境，并强调了设计可信赖、情感共鸣的数字心理健康工具的启示。

### [114] [CellScout: Visual Analytics for Mining Biomarkers in Cell State Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03485)
*Rui Sheng,Zelin Zang,Jiachen Wang,Yan Luo,Zixin Chen,Yan Zhou,Shaolun Ruan,Huamin Qu*

Main category: cs.HC

TL;DR: CellScout是一个可视化分析系统，通过机器学习算法识别细胞群体与生物标志物之间的关联关系，帮助生物学家更有效地发现细胞状态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 细胞状态发现对理解生物系统和改善医疗结果至关重要，但当前方法存在缺陷：生物学家通常通过降维可视化将视觉上聚类的细胞视为不同状态，然后寻找独特的生物标志物。然而，由于聚类内部的不一致性，这种方法往往是试错性的且高度不确定，生物学家急需有效工具来揭示细胞群体与潜在生物标志物之间的隐藏关联关系。

Method: 首先设计了一个基于专家混合（Mixture-of-Experts, MoE）技术的机器学习算法，用于识别细胞群体与生物标志物之间有意义的关联关系。然后与生物学家合作开发了可视化分析系统CellScout，帮助探索和优化这些关联关系以推进细胞状态发现。

Result: 通过专家访谈验证了系统有效性，并选择了一个代表性案例来展示其在发现新细胞状态方面的能力。系统能够帮助生物学家更准确地识别定义特定细胞状态的独特生物标志物。

Conclusion: CellScout通过结合机器学习算法和可视化分析，解决了细胞状态与生物标志物共同发现过程中的挑战，为生物学家提供了有效的工具来探索细胞群体与生物标志物之间的关联关系，从而推进细胞状态发现。

Abstract: Cell state discovery is crucial for understanding biological systems and enhancing medical outcomes. A key aspect of this process is identifying distinct biomarkers that define specific cell states. However, difficulties arise from the co-discovery process of cell states and biomarkers: biologists often use dimensionality reduction to visualize cells in a two- dimensional space. Then they usually interpret visually clustered cells as distinct states, from which they seek to identify unique biomarkers. However, this assumption is often invalid due to internal inconsistencies in a cluster, making the process trial-and-error and highly uncertain. Therefore, biologists urgently need effective tools to help uncover the hidden association relationships between different cell populations and their potential biomarkers. To address this problem, we first designed a machine-learning algorithm based on the Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) technique to identify meaningful associations between cell populations and biomarkers. We further developed a visual analytics system, CellScout, in collaboration with biologists, to help them explore and refine these association relationships to advance cell state discovery. We validated our system through expert interviews, from which we further selected a representative case to demonstrate its effectiveness in discovering new cell states.

中文标题: CellScout：用于挖掘细胞状态发现中生物标志物的可视化分析

中文摘要: 细胞状态发现对于理解生物系统和改善医疗结果至关重要。这一过程的关键方面是识别定义特定细胞状态的独特生物标志物。然而，细胞状态和生物标志物的共同发现过程存在困难：生物学家通常使用降维技术将细胞可视化在二维空间中。然后他们通常将视觉上聚类的细胞解释为不同的状态，并从中寻找独特的生物标志物。然而，由于聚类内部的不一致性，这种假设通常是无效的，使得该过程成为试错性的且高度不确定。因此，生物学家迫切需要有效的工具来帮助揭示不同细胞群体与其潜在生物标志物之间的隐藏关联关系。为了解决这个问题，我们首先设计了一个基于专家混合（MoE）技术的机器学习算法，用于识别细胞群体与生物标志物之间有意义的关联关系。我们进一步与生物学家合作开发了一个可视化分析系统CellScout，帮助他们探索和优化这些关联关系以推进细胞状态发现。我们通过专家访谈验证了我们的系统，并从中选择了一个代表性案例来展示其在发现新细胞状态方面的有效性。

### [115] [EMINDS: Understanding User Behavior Progression for Mental Health Exploration on Social Media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03495)
*Rui Sheng,Yifang Wang,Xingbo Wang,Shun Dai,Qingyu Guo,Tai-Quan Peng,Huamin Qu,Dongyu Liu*

Main category: cs.HC

TL;DR: EMINDS是一个可视化分析系统，用于探索社交媒体上用户心理健康相关的行为进展，通过自动挖掘管道提取不同行为阶段，并评估频繁阶段模式对心理健康状态的潜在长期影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 心理健康是一个紧迫的社会问题，研究人员越来越多地利用在线心理健康社区分析用户行为数据进行早期干预。然而，现有的序列挖掘技术无法满足探索不同群体（如恢复或恶化群体）行为进展以及追踪行为对心理健康状态潜在长期影响的迫切需求。

Method: EMINDS基于新颖的自动挖掘管道构建，该管道提取不同的行为阶段，并评估频繁阶段模式随时间对心理健康状态的潜在影响。系统包含一组交互式可视化，总结每个行为阶段的含义和不同阶段模式的演变。特别设计了以模式为中心的桑基图，揭示阶段模式对心理健康影响的上下文信息。

Result: 通过两个案例研究和专家访谈评估了EMINDS的有效性和可用性，通过分析Reddit上的用户行为，检验了可能影响长期心理健康的潜在阶段模式。系统帮助专家理解阶段模式前后序列的具体变化。

Conclusion: EMINDS能够有效探索社交媒体用户的行为进展，识别影响心理健康的模式，为心理健康研究和早期干预提供有价值的分析工具。

Abstract: Mental health is an urgent societal issue, and social scientists are increasingly turning to online mental health communities (OMHCs) to analyze user behavior data for early intervention. However, existing sequence mining techniques fall short of the urgent need to explore the behavior progression of different groups (e.g., recovery or deterioration groups) and track the potential long-term impact of behaviors on mental health status. To address this issue, we introduce EMINDS, a visual analytics system built on a novel automatic mining pipeline that extracts distinct behavior stages and assesses the potential impact of frequent stage patterns on mental health status over time. The system includes a set of interactive visualizations that summarize the meaning of each behavior stage and the evolution of different stage patterns. We feature a pattern-centric Sankey diagram to reveal contextual information about the impact of stage patterns on mental health, helping experts understand the specific changes in sequences before and after a stage pattern. We evaluated the effectiveness and usability of EMINDS through two case studies and expert interviews, which examined the potential stage patterns impacting long-term mental health by analyzing user behaviors on Reddit.

中文标题: EMINDS：理解社交媒体上用户心理健康探索的行为进展

中文摘要: 心理健康是一个紧迫的社会问题，社会科学家越来越多地转向在线心理健康社区（OMHCs）分析用户行为数据以进行早期干预。然而，现有的序列挖掘技术无法满足探索不同群体（如恢复或恶化群体）行为进展以及追踪行为对心理健康状态潜在长期影响的迫切需求。为解决这一问题，我们引入了EMINDS，这是一个基于新颖自动挖掘管道构建的可视化分析系统，该系统提取不同的行为阶段，并评估频繁阶段模式随时间对心理健康状态的潜在影响。该系统包括一组交互式可视化，总结每个行为阶段的含义和不同阶段模式的演变。我们设计了一个以模式为中心的桑基图，揭示阶段模式对心理健康影响的上下文信息，帮助专家理解阶段模式前后序列的具体变化。我们通过两个案例研究和专家访谈评估了EMINDS的有效性和可用性，通过分析Reddit上的用户行为，检验了可能影响长期心理健康的潜在阶段模式。

### [116] [Left shifting analysis of Human-Autonomous Team interactions to analyse risks of autonomy in high-stakes AI systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03519)
*Ben Larwood,Oliver J. Sutton,Callum Cockburn*

Main category: cs.HC

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种"左移"框架，用于早期识别高风险AI系统中人机自主协作的故障风险，基于LaMonica的人机团队模型，通过分析交互故障模式来增强系统稳健性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开发高风险自主AI系统面临复杂挑战：错误后果严重，但难以预测所有操作情况。在时间紧迫等压力场景下，故障风险加剧。当前缺乏对AI故障模式的理解，阻碍了AI在智能系统中的稳健应用，导致项目风险、时间和成本增加。

Method: 提出基于系统工程"左移"原则的框架，将AI故障分析提前到设计阶段。核心是基于LaMonica等人（2022）的人机自主团队模型，分析人类与自主系统之间的交互，系统识别操作领域中的人机交互风险，覆盖整个操作设计域。

Result: 该方法能够早期表征人机自主协作中出现的风险，增强系统稳健性。通过指挥与控制（C2）系统AI助手的示例用例进行了实际演示。

Conclusion: 将AI故障模式分析纳入系统生命周期的早期设计阶段至关重要。提出的"左移"框架通过系统分析人机交互风险，能够提高高风险AI系统的稳健性和可靠性，减少项目风险、时间和成本。

Abstract: Developing high-stakes autonomous systems that include Artificial Intelligence (AI) components is complex; the consequences of errors can be catastrophic, yet it is challenging to plan for all operational cases. In stressful scenarios for the human operator, such as short decision-making timescales, the risk of failures is exacerbated. A lack of understanding of AI failure modes obstructs this and so blocks the robust implementation of applications of AI in smart systems. This prevents early risk identification, leading to increased time, risk and cost of projects.
  A key tenet of Systems Engineering and acquisition engineering is centred around a "left-shift" in test and evaluation activities to earlier in the system lifecycle, to allow for "accelerated delivery of [systems] that work". We argue it is therefore essential that this shift includes the analysis of AI failure cases as part of the design stages of the system life cycle. Our proposed framework enables the early characterisation of risks emerging from human-autonomy teaming (HAT) in operational contexts. The cornerstone of this is a new analysis of AI failure modes, built on the seminal modelling of human-autonomy teams laid out by LaMonica et al., 2022. Using the analysis of the interactions between human and autonomous systems and exploring the failure modes within each aspect, our approach provides a way to systematically identify human-AI interactions risks across the operational domain of the system of interest. The understanding of the emergent behaviour enables increased robustness of the system, for which the analysis should be undertaken over the whole scope of its operational design domain. This approach is illustrated through an example use case for an AI assistant supporting a Command & Control (C2) System.

中文标题: 人机自主团队交互的左移分析：高风险AI系统中自主性风险分析

中文摘要: 开发包含人工智能组件的高风险自主系统是复杂的；错误的后果可能是灾难性的，但为所有操作情况制定计划具有挑战性。在人类操作员面临压力的情况下，例如决策时间紧迫，故障风险会加剧。对AI故障模式缺乏理解阻碍了这一点，从而阻碍了AI在智能系统中的稳健应用。这妨碍了早期风险识别，导致项目时间、风险和成本增加。

系统工程和采办工程的一个关键原则是围绕测试和评估活动的"左移"，将其提前到系统生命周期的早期阶段，以实现"加速交付[有效工作的系统]"。我们认为，这种转变必须包括将AI故障案例分析作为系统生命周期设计阶段的一部分。我们提出的框架能够早期表征在操作环境中人机自主协作（HAT）中出现的风险。其核心是基于LaMonica等人（2022年）建立的人机自主团队建模基础，对AI故障模式进行新的分析。通过分析人类与自主系统之间的交互，并探索每个方面的故障模式，我们的方法提供了一种系统识别感兴趣系统操作领域中的人机交互风险的方法。对涌现行为的理解增强了系统的稳健性，该分析应在其整个操作设计域范围内进行。该方法通过一个支持指挥与控制（C2）系统的AI助手示例用例进行说明。

### [117] [Synthetic Cognitive Walkthrough: Aligning Large Language Model Performance with Human Cognitive Walkthrough](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03568)
*Ruican Zhong,David W. McDonald,Gary Hsieh*

Main category: cs.HC

TL;DR: LLMs可以模拟认知走查，但行为与人类不同：任务完成率更高、路径更优，但识别失败点较少。通过额外提示，LLMs可以预测人类识别的失败点，与人类表现对齐。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 认知走查等可用性测试成本高昂，而具备视觉推理和UI导航能力的大语言模型为自动化认知走查提供了机会。研究探索LLMs是否能模拟人类在认知走查中的行为。

Method: 比较GPT-4和Gemini-2.5-pro与人类参与者在认知走查中的表现，分析任务完成率、导航路径和失败点识别。通过后续研究测试额外提示是否能改善LLMs预测人类识别失败点的能力。

Result: LLMs能够导航界面并提供合理推理，但行为与人类不同：LLM提示的认知走查任务完成率高于人类，遵循更优导航路径，但识别潜在失败点较少。通过额外提示，LLMs可以预测人类识别的失败点，使其表现与人类参与者对齐。

Conclusion: 虽然LLMs不能完全复制人类行为，但可以用于扩展可用性走查和提供UI洞察，作为传统可用性测试的有价值补充。

Abstract: Conducting usability testing like cognitive walkthrough (CW) can be costly. Recent developments in large language models (LLMs), with visual reasoning and UI navigation capabilities, present opportunities to automate CW. We explored whether LLMs (GPT-4 and Gemini-2.5-pro) can simulate human behavior in CW by comparing their walkthroughs with human participants. While LLMs could navigate interfaces and provide reasonable rationales, their behavior differed from humans. LLM-prompted CW achieved higher task completion rates than humans and followed more optimal navigation paths, while identifying fewer potential failure points. However, follow-up studies demonstrated that with additional prompting, LLMs can predict human-identified failure points, aligning their performance with human participants. Our work highlights that while LLMs may not replicate human behaviors exactly, they can be leveraged for scaling usability walkthroughs and providing UI insights, offering a valuable complement to traditional usability testing.

中文标题: 合成认知走查：将大语言模型表现与人类认知走查对齐

中文摘要: 进行认知走查等可用性测试可能成本高昂。最近具备视觉推理和UI导航能力的大语言模型的发展为自动化认知走查提供了机会。我们通过比较LLMs（GPT-4和Gemini-2.5-pro）与人类参与者的走查，探索了LLMs是否能模拟人类在认知走查中的行为。虽然LLMs能够导航界面并提供合理推理，但其行为与人类不同。LLM提示的认知走查实现了比人类更高的任务完成率，并遵循更优的导航路径，同时识别出较少的潜在失败点。然而，后续研究表明，通过额外提示，LLMs可以预测人类识别的失败点，使其表现与人类参与者对齐。我们的工作强调，虽然LLMs可能无法完全复制人类行为，但它们可以用于扩展可用性走查和提供UI洞察，为传统可用性测试提供有价值的补充。

### [118] [Sleep Modulation: The Challenge of Transitioning from Open Loop to Closed Loop](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03784)
*Guisong Liu,Jiansong Zhang,Yinpei Luo,Guoliang Wei,Shuqing Sun,Shiyang Deng,Pengfei Wei,Nanxi Chen*

Main category: cs.HC

TL;DR: 睡眠调制研究正从开环范式向闭环系统转型，以解决个体适应性和调制精度不足的问题，推动临床应用和家庭部署。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 睡眠障碍已成为全球性健康问题，急需有效且广泛可及的干预技术。当前多数睡眠调制研究依赖经验参数的开环范式，缺乏个体适应性和调制精度，限制了临床转化和家庭环境的大规模部署。

Method: 本文首先界定了睡眠调制的基本范式，批判性分析了开环方法的内在局限性，并正式概念化了睡眠闭环调制。然后综合评述了五种常用调制技术的研究，评估它们在闭环框架中的整合潜力。最后识别了构建有效睡眠闭环调制系统的三大挑战：传感器方案选择、监测模型设计和调制策略设计，并提出了潜在解决方案。

Result: 通过系统分析，本文明确了从开环向闭环转型的必要性，提出了闭环系统的理论框架，并识别了实现这一转型的关键技术挑战和潜在解决路径。

Conclusion: 睡眠调制领域正面临从开环范式向闭环系统的范式转变，这需要解决传感器、监测模型和调制策略三大核心挑战。闭环系统有望实现个体化、自适应的睡眠调制，从而推动临床转化和家庭环境的大规模应用。

Abstract: Sleep disorders have emerged as a critical global health issue, highlighting the urgent need for effective and widely accessible intervention technologies. Non-invasive brain stimulation has garnered attention as it enables direct or indirect modulation of neural activity, thereby promoting sleep enhancement in a safe and unobtrusive manner. This class of approaches is collectively referred to as sleep modulation. To date, the majority of sleep modulation research relies on open-loop paradigms with empirically determined parameters, while achieving individual adaptation and modulation accuracy remains a distant objective. The paradigm-specific constraints inherent to open-loop designs represent a major obstacle to clinical translation and large-scale deployment in home environments. In this paper, we delineate fundamental paradigms of sleep modulation, critically examine the intrinsic limitations of open-loop approaches, and formally conceptualize sleep closed-loop modulation. We further provide a comprehensive synthesis of prior studies involving five commonly employed modulation techniques, evaluating their potential integration within a closed-loop framework. Finally, we identify three primary challenges in constructing an effective sleep closed-loop modulation system: sensor solution selection, monitoring model design, and modulation strategy design, while also proposing potential solutions. Collectively, this work aims to advance the paradigm shift of sleep modulation from open-loop toward closed-loop systems.

中文标题: 睡眠调制：从开环到闭环转型的挑战

中文摘要: 睡眠障碍已成为关键的全球健康问题，凸显了对有效且广泛可及的干预技术的迫切需求。非侵入性脑刺激因其能够直接或间接调节神经活动，从而以安全、无干扰的方式促进睡眠改善而受到关注。这类方法统称为睡眠调制。迄今为止，大多数睡眠调制研究依赖于经验参数确定的开环范式，而实现个体适应性和调制精度仍然是一个遥远的目标。开环设计固有的范式特定限制是临床转化和家庭环境大规模部署的主要障碍。在本文中，我们界定了睡眠调制的基本范式，批判性地审视了开环方法的内在局限性，并正式概念化了睡眠闭环调制。我们进一步综合评述了涉及五种常用调制技术的前期研究，评估它们在闭环框架中的整合潜力。最后，我们识别了构建有效睡眠闭环调制系统的三大主要挑战：传感器方案选择、监测模型设计和调制策略设计，同时提出了潜在解决方案。总体而言，这项工作旨在推动睡眠调制从开环向闭环系统的范式转变。

### [119] [Adhera: A Human-Centered Health Informatics Solution for Reducing Informal Caregiver Burden through Improved Medication Adherence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03878)
*Zhiyin Zhou*

Main category: cs.HC

TL;DR: Adhera是一个包含照护者的健康信息系统，通过智能药盒和移动应用改善药物依从性，减轻照护者负担。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 全球老龄化加剧和医疗人员短缺导致对非正式照护者依赖增加，药物管理是照护者最繁重且易出错的任务之一。现有数字健康解决方案大多只关注患者，忽视了照护者的信息和情感需求，导致照护者压力增大。

Method: 采用混合方法研究设计：15次半结构化照护者访谈、65份调查回复、5次药剂师咨询。基于CeHRes路线图2.0和TBLD+C框架，结合协同设计研究，开发了配备传感器的智能药盒和移动应用系统。

Result: 初步评估显示Adhera增强了药物管理的可视性，提高了照护者信心，简化了药物管理流程。系统能够记录摄入事件、发送实时提醒，为照护者提供同步依从性数据。

Conclusion: Adhera通过以人为本的设计和协作框架，将技术创新与同理心驱动的护理相结合，为减轻照护者负担提供了有效解决方案，为健康信息学领域做出了贡献。

Abstract: The growing global population of older adults, combined with ongoing healthcare workforce shortages, has increased reliance on informal caregivers, including family members and friends who provide unpaid support to individuals with chronic illnesses. Among their daily responsibilities, medication management remains one of the most demanding and error-prone tasks. Non-adherence to prescribed regimens not only undermines patient outcomes but also intensifies caregiver stress, anxiety, and fatigue. Although digital health technologies have proliferated to address adherence, most solutions focus exclusively on patients and neglect the informational and emotional needs of caregivers. This paper introduces Adhera, a caregiver-inclusive health informatics system designed to support medication adherence while reducing caregiver burden. Using a mixed-methods research design that included fifteen semi-structured caregiver interviews, sixty-five survey responses, and five pharmacist consultations, this study identified three primary challenges: caregiver stress related to uncertainty about medication intake, fragmented communication with healthcare professionals, and distrust in existing digital tools. Informed by the CeHRes Roadmap 2.0 and the Triple Bottom Line by Design and Culture (TBLD+C) framework, as well as recent co-design studies involving caregivers, Adhera integrates a sensor-equipped smart pill organizer with a mobile companion application that records intake events, sends real-time reminders, and provides caregivers with synchronized adherence data. Preliminary evaluation suggests that Adhera enhances visibility, improves caregiver confidence, and streamlines medication routines. This study contributes to the field of health informatics by demonstrating how human-centered design and collaborative frameworks can align technical innovation with empathy-driven care.

中文标题: Adhera：一种以人为本的健康信息学解决方案，通过改善药物依从性减轻非正式照护者负担

中文摘要: 全球老年人口不断增长，加上持续的医疗保健劳动力短缺，增加了对非正式照护者的依赖，包括为慢性病患者提供无偿支持的家人和朋友。在他们的日常职责中，药物管理仍然是最具挑战性和最容易出错的任务之一。不遵守处方方案不仅影响患者治疗效果，还会加剧照护者的压力、焦虑和疲劳。尽管数字健康技术已经大量涌现以解决依从性问题，但大多数解决方案仅关注患者，而忽视了照护者的信息和情感需求。本文介绍了Adhera，一种包含照护者的健康信息系统，旨在支持药物依从性同时减轻照护者负担。通过采用混合方法研究设计，包括十五次半结构化照护者访谈、六十五份调查回复和五次药剂师咨询，本研究确定了三个主要挑战：与药物摄入不确定性相关的照护者压力、与医疗专业人员沟通不畅以及对现有数字工具的不信任。基于CeHRes路线图2.0和设计与文化三重底线（TBLD+C）框架，以及最近涉及照护者的协同设计研究，Adhera整合了配备传感器的智能药盒和移动伴侣应用程序，记录摄入事件、发送实时提醒，并为照护者提供同步的依从性数据。初步评估表明，Adhera增强了可视性，提高了照护者信心，并简化了药物管理流程。本研究通过展示以人为本的设计和协作框架如何将技术创新与同理心驱动的护理相结合，为健康信息学领域做出了贡献。

### [120] [HEART-Watch: A multimodal physiological dataset from a Google Pixel Watch across different physical states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03988)
*Jathushan Kaetheeswaran,Boyi Ma,Ali Abedi,Milad Lankarany,Shehroz Khan*

Main category: cs.HC

TL;DR: HEART-Watch是一个多模态生理数据集，包含来自40名健康成年人在坐、站、走三种状态下同步采集的Google Pixel Watch 2心电图、光电容积描记和加速度计信号，以及参考胸导心电图，旨在支持消费级智能手表心血管分析算法的开发和基准测试。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 心血管疾病是全球主要死亡原因，消费级智能手表为大众提供了新的个性化健康监测选择。然而，现有公开的消费级智能手表数据集缺乏同步心血管生物信号和丰富的人口多样性，导致算法开发可能存在偏差。

Method: 从40名健康成年人收集数据，使用Google Pixel Watch 2同步采集手腕佩戴的心电图、光电容积描记和加速度计信号，覆盖坐、站、走三种物理状态，同时采集参考胸导心电图作为对照，并收集间歇性上臂血压测量数据作为额外生物标志物。

Result: 创建了一个包含多模态生理信号的数据集，包括同步的智能手表生物信号和参考心电图，为消费级智能手表心血管监测算法的开发和验证提供了现实数据基础。

Conclusion: HEART-Watch数据集旨在支持跨多样化人群的消费级智能手表心血管分析算法的开发和基准测试，促进更可靠、无偏的心血管监测算法发展。

Abstract: Consumer-grade smartwatches offer a new personalized health monitoring option for general consumers globally as cardiovascular diseases continue to prevail as the leading cause of global mortality. The development and validation of reliable cardiovascular monitoring algorithms for these consumer-grade devices requires realistic biosignal data from diverse sets of participants. However, the availability of public consumer-grade smartwatch datasets with synchronized cardiovascular biosignals is limited, and existing datasets do not offer rich demographic diversity in their participant cohorts, leading to potentially biased algorithm development. This paper presents HEART-Watch, a multimodal physiological dataset collected from temporally synchronized wrist-worn Google Pixel Watch 2 electrocardiogram (ECG), photoplethysmography, and accelerometer signals from a diverse cohort of 40 healthy adults across three physical states - sitting, standing and walking with reference chest ECG. Intermittent upper arm blood pressure measurements and concurrent biosignals were collected as an additional biomarker for future research. The motivation, methodology, and initial analyses of results are presented. HEART-Watch is intended to support the development and benchmarking of robust algorithms for cardiovascular analyses on consumer-grade smartwatches across diverse populations.

中文标题: HEART-Watch：基于Google Pixel Watch在不同生理状态下采集的多模态生理数据集

中文摘要: 随着心血管疾病持续成为全球主要死亡原因，消费级智能手表为全球普通消费者提供了新的个性化健康监测选择。为这些消费级设备开发和验证可靠的心血管监测算法需要来自多样化参与者的现实生物信号数据。然而，具有同步心血管生物信号的公开消费级智能手表数据集有限，现有数据集在其参与者群体中未提供丰富的人口多样性，可能导致算法开发存在偏差。本文介绍了HEART-Watch，这是一个从40名健康成年人多样化群体中收集的多模态生理数据集，包含时间同步的手腕佩戴Google Pixel Watch 2心电图、光电容积描记和加速度计信号，覆盖坐、站、走三种物理状态，并配有参考胸导心电图。间歇性上臂血压测量和并发生物信号作为未来研究的额外生物标志物被收集。本文介绍了研究动机、方法论和初步分析结果。HEART-Watch旨在支持跨多样化人群的消费级智能手表心血管分析算法的开发和基准测试。

### [121] [Comparing Unsupervised and Supervised Semantic Speech Tokens: A Case Study of Child ASR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03301)
*Mohan Shi,Natarajan Balaji Shankar,Kaiyuan Zhang,Zilai Wang,Abeer Alwan*

Main category: eess.AS

TL;DR: 本文系统比较了监督和无监督语义语音标记在儿童ASR中的表现，发现监督方法不仅优于无监督方法，甚至意外超越了连续表示，在超低比特率设置下也表现良好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 离散语音标记因其存储效率和与大型语言模型的集成而受到关注。语义标记比声学标记在自动语音识别中更有优势。传统上使用无监督K-means聚类从语音基础模型中提取语义标记，而最近出现了使用ASR损失训练的监督方法。本文旨在系统比较这两种方法在儿童ASR这一低资源任务中的表现。

Method: 本研究比较了两种语义语音标记提取方法：1）无监督K-means聚类方法，从预训练语音基础模型中提取语义标记；2）监督方法，使用有限标量量化（FSQ）并结合ASR损失进行训练。两种方法都利用了预训练的语音基础模型，并在儿童ASR任务上进行系统评估。

Result: 实验结果表明：1）监督方法在儿童ASR任务上明显优于无监督方法；2）监督方法甚至意外地超越了连续表示的性能；3）监督方法在超低比特率设置下仍然表现良好。

Conclusion: 监督语义语音标记在儿童ASR中具有显著优势，不仅优于无监督方法，甚至超越了连续表示。这些发现突出了监督语义标记的优越性，并为改进离散语音标记化提供了重要见解。

Abstract: Discrete speech tokens have gained attention for their storage efficiency and integration with Large Language Models (LLMs). They are commonly categorized into acoustic and semantic tokens, with the latter being more advantageous for Automatic Speech Recognition (ASR). Traditionally, unsupervised K-means clustering has been used to extract semantic speech tokens from Speech Foundation Models (SFMs). Recently, supervised methods, such as finite scalar quantization (FSQ) trained with ASR loss, have emerged for speech generation. Both approaches leverage pre-trained SFMs, benefiting low-resource tasks such as child ASR.
  This paper systematically compares supervised and unsupervised semantic speech tokens for child ASR. Results show that supervised methods not only outperform unsupervised ones but even unexpectedly surpass continuous representations, and they perform well even in ultra-low bitrate settings. These findings highlight the advantages of supervised semantic tokens and offer insights for improving discrete speech tokenization.

中文标题: 比较无监督与监督语义语音标记：儿童自动语音识别案例研究

中文摘要: 离散语音标记因其存储效率和与大型语言模型的集成而受到关注。它们通常分为声学标记和语义标记，其中语义标记在自动语音识别中更具优势。传统上使用无监督K-means聚类从语音基础模型中提取语义语音标记。最近，出现了监督方法，例如使用ASR损失训练的有限标量量化用于语音生成。两种方法都利用了预训练的语音基础模型，有利于低资源任务如儿童ASR。

### [122] [A Universal Harmonic Discriminator for High-quality GAN-based Vocoder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03486)
*Nan Xu,Zhaolong Huang,Xiao Zeng*

Main category: eess.AS

TL;DR: 提出一种通用的谐波判别器，通过可学习的三角带通滤波器组实现动态频率分辨率建模和谐波跟踪，提升GAN声码器的音质


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的STFT频谱图在不同频率段具有相同的频率分辨率，这导致性能不佳，特别是在处理歌声时。为了解决这个问题，需要设计一个能够动态调整频率分辨率并跟踪谐波的判别器。

Method: 设计了一个谐波滤波器，使用可学习的三角带通滤波器组，每个频率段具有灵活的带宽。此外，添加了半谐波来捕捉低频段的细粒度谐波关系。

Result: 在语音和歌声数据集上的实验验证了所提判别器在主观和客观指标上的有效性。

Conclusion: 提出的通用谐波判别器通过动态频率分辨率建模和谐波跟踪，显著提升了基于GAN的声码器的音质。

Abstract: With the emergence of GAN-based vocoders, the discriminator, as a crucial component, has been developed recently. In our work, we focus on improving the time-frequency based discriminator. Particularly, Short-Time Fourier Transform (STFT) representation is usually used as input of time-frequency based discriminator. However, the STFT spectrogram has the same frequency resolution at different frequency bins, which results in an inferior performance, especially for singing voices. Motivated by this, we propose a universal harmonic discriminator for dynamic frequency resolution modeling and harmonic tracking. Specifically, we design a harmonic filter with learnable triangular band-pass filter banks, where each frequency bin has a flexible bandwidth. Additionally, we add a half-harmonic to capture fine-grained harmonic relationships at low-frequency band. Experiments on speech and singing datasets validate the effectiveness of the proposed discriminator on both subjective and objective metrics.

### [123] [On the Complexity of the Ordered Covering Problem in Distance Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03124)
*Michael Souza,Júlio Araújo,John Kesley Costa,Carlile Lavor*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文证明了有序覆盖问题（OCP）是NP完全的，通过从3-划分问题的归约，为蛋白质结构确定中的边排序问题建立了计算复杂性理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有序覆盖问题（OCP）在蛋白质结构确定的DMDGP问题中至关重要，因为剪枝边的排序显著影响SBBU算法的性能。虽然已有启发式算法表现出色，但寻找最优解的计算复杂性一直未解决，需要理论分析来确定问题的固有难度。

Method: 采用计算复杂性理论分析方法，通过多项式时间归约从强NP完全问题3-划分问题到OCP问题，构造严格的预算约束来证明OCP的NP完全性。

Result: 成功证明了有序覆盖问题是NP完全的，为最优边排序问题建立了计算障碍，解释了为什么启发式方法是实践中必要的选择。

Conclusion: OCP的NP完全性为蛋白质结构确定中的边排序问题提供了理论解释，支持了当前启发式方法的合理性，并表明寻找最优解在计算上是困难的。

Abstract: The Ordered Covering Problem (OCP) arises in the context of the Discretizable Molecular Distance Geometry Problem (DMDGP), where the ordering of pruning edges significantly impacts the performance of the SBBU algorithm for protein structure determination. In recent work, Souza et al. (2023) formalized OCP as a hypergraph covering problem with ordered, exponential costs, and proposed a greedy heuristic that outperforms the original SBBU ordering by orders of magnitude. However, the computational complexity of finding optimal solutions remained open. In this paper, we prove that OCP is NP-complete through a polynomial-time reduction from the strongly NP-complete 3-Partition problem. Our reduction constructs a tight budget that forces optimal solutions to correspond exactly to valid 3-partitions. This result establishes a computational barrier for optimal edge ordering and provides theoretical justification for the heuristic approaches currently used in practice.

中文标题: 距离几何中有序覆盖问题的复杂性分析

中文摘要: 有序覆盖问题（OCP）出现在可离散化分子距离几何问题（DMDGP）的背景下，其中剪枝边的排序显著影响蛋白质结构确定中SBBU算法的性能。在最近的工作中，Souza等人（2023）将OCP形式化为具有有序、指数成本超图覆盖问题，并提出了一种贪心启发式算法，其性能比原始SBBU排序高出几个数量级。然而，寻找最优解的计算复杂性仍然未解决。在本文中，我们通过从强NP完全问题3-划分问题的多项式时间归约，证明了OCP是NP完全的。我们的归约构造了一个严格的预算约束，迫使最优解恰好对应于有效的3-划分。这一结果为最优边排序建立了计算障碍，并为当前实践中使用的启发式方法提供了理论依据。

</details>


### [124] [Complexity of Local Search for CSPs Parameterized by Constraint Difference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03275)
*Aditya Anand,Vincent Cohen-Addad,Tommaso d'Orsi,Anupam Gupta,Euiwoong Lee,Debmalya Panigrahi,Sijin Peng*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文研究了CSP局部搜索的参数化复杂性，提出了基于当前解与最优解差异距离k的新参数化模型，并对布尔对称CSPs的复杂性进行了完整分类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 局部搜索是解决优化问题的常用启发式方法，但对其参数化复杂性的理论研究相对缺乏。本文旨在建立局部搜索的参数化复杂性理论框架，特别是针对约束满足问题，通过引入当前解与最优解之间的差异距离作为参数，为局部搜索算法提供理论保证。

Method: 提出基于差异距离的参数化局部搜索模型，将当前解P与最优解S*的对称差|PΔS*|作为参数k。将该模型应用于布尔对称CSPs，通过分析谓词特性（接受真文字数量）来分类问题的参数化复杂性。使用参数化复杂性理论工具，如固定参数可处理性（FPT）和W[1]-硬度等。

Result: 对布尔对称CSPs的局部搜索参数化复杂性给出了完整分类：某些问题在FPT类中（如Max-Cut），而其他问题则是W[1]-难的（如Max-3SAT）。分类结果基于谓词的单调性和其他组合特性。

Conclusion: 局部搜索的参数化复杂性高度依赖于基础优化问题的结构特性。对于布尔对称CSPs，可以通过谓词的组合特性预测其局部搜索的复杂性。该框架为设计具有理论保证的局部搜索算法提供了基础，并揭示了哪些问题可以通过参数化方法有效解决。

Abstract: In this paper, we study the parameterized complexity of local search, whose goal is to find a good nearby solution from the given current solution. Formally, given an optimization problem where the goal is to find the largest feasible subset $S$ of a universe $U$, the new input consists of a current solution $P$ (not necessarily feasible) as well as an ordinary input for the problem.
  Given the existence of a feasible solution $S^*$, the goal is to find a feasible solution as good as $S^*$ in parameterized time $f(k) \cdot n^{O(1)}$, where $k$ denotes the distance $|PΔS^*|$. This model generalizes numerous classical parameterized optimization problems whose parameter $k$ is the minimum number of elements removed from $U$ to make it feasible, which corresponds to the case $P = U$.
  We apply this model to widely studied Constraint Satisfaction Problems (CSPs), where $U$ is the set of constraints, and a subset $U'$ of constraints is feasible if there is an assignment to the variables satisfying all constraints in $U'$. We give a complete characterization of the parameterized complexity of all boolean-alphabet symmetric CSPs, where the predicate's acceptance depends on the number of true literals.

中文标题: 基于约束差异参数化的CSP局部搜索复杂性

中文摘要: 本文研究了局部搜索的参数化复杂性，其目标是从给定的当前解中找到一个良好的邻近解。形式上，给定一个优化问题，目标是找到宇宙U的最大可行子集S，新输入包括当前解P（不一定可行）以及问题的普通输入。给定存在可行解S*的情况下，目标是在参数化时间f(k)·n^O(1)内找到与S*一样好的可行解，其中k表示距离|PΔS*|。该模型推广了众多经典参数化优化问题，其参数k是从U中移除以使其可行的最小元素数量，这对应于P=U的情况。我们将此模型应用于广泛研究的约束满足问题（CSPs），其中U是约束集合，约束子集U'是可行的，如果存在对变量的赋值满足U'中的所有约束。我们对所有布尔字母表对称CSPs的参数化复杂性给出了完整的刻画，其中谓词的接受取决于真文字的数量。

</details>


### [125] [Fast approximate $\ell$-center clustering in high dimensional spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03304)
*Mirosław Kowaluk,Andrzej Lingas,Mia Persson*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 该论文提出使用随机降维技术加速高维空间中的ℓ-中心聚类和最小直径ℓ-聚类问题的近似算法，显著提高了计算效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高维空间中，ℓ-中心聚类和最小直径ℓ-聚类问题的传统算法计算复杂度高，特别是当ℓ和维度都很大时。需要开发更高效的近似算法来应对高维数据的挑战。

Method: 主要采用随机降维技术：1）提出通用方法减少算法对维度大小的依赖；2）基于此方法设计(2+ε)-近似算法；3）将方法应用于现有更高近似保证的算法；4）为包含异常值的ℓ-中心聚类问题提供加速方法。

Result: 1）开发了比已知2-近似算法更快的(2+ε)-近似算法；2）当ℓ和维度都是超对数时，算法性能显著提升；3）为包含异常值的ℓ-中心聚类问题提供了加速的O(1)-近似方法。

Conclusion: 随机降维是解决高维空间中聚类问题计算复杂度的有效工具，能够显著提高近似算法的效率，特别是在ℓ和维度都很大的情况下，为高维数据聚类提供了实用的解决方案。

Abstract: We study the design of efficient approximation algorithms for the
  $\ell$-center clustering and minimum-diameter $\ell$-clustering
  problems in high dimensional Euclidean and Hamming spaces. Our main
  tool is randomized dimension reduction. First, we present a general
  method of reducing the dependency of the running time of a
  hypothetical algorithm for the $\ell$-center problem in a high
  dimensional Euclidean space on the dimension size. Utilizing in
  part this method, we provide $(2+ε)$- approximation
  algorithms for the $\ell$-center clustering and minimum-diameter
  $\ell$-clustering problems in Euclidean and Hamming spaces that are
  substantially faster than the known $2$-approximation ones when both
  $\ell$ and the dimension are super-logarithmic. Next, we apply the
  general method to the recent fast approximation algorithms with
  higher approximation guarantees for the $\ell$-center clustering
  problem in a high dimensional Euclidean space. Finally, we provide a
  speed-up of the known $O(1)$-approximation method for the
  generalization of the $\ell$-center clustering problem to include
  $z$ outliers (i.e., $z$ input points can be ignored while computing
  the maximum distance of an input point to a center) in high
  dimensional Euclidean and Hamming spaces.

中文标题: 高维空间中的快速近似$\ell$-中心聚类

中文摘要: 我们研究了在高维欧几里得空间和汉明空间中设计$\ell$-中心聚类和最小直径$\ell$-聚类问题的高效近似算法。我们的主要工具是随机降维。首先，我们提出了一种通用方法，用于减少高维欧几里得空间中$\ell$-中心问题假设算法运行时间对维度大小的依赖性。利用这种方法，我们为欧几里得空间和汉明空间中的$\ell$-中心聚类和最小直径$\ell$-聚类问题提供了$(2+ε)$-近似算法，当$\ell$和维度都是超对数时，这些算法比已知的$2$-近似算法快得多。接下来，我们将通用方法应用于最近针对高维欧几里得空间中$\ell$-中心聚类问题的具有更高近似保证的快速近似算法。最后，我们为$\ell$-中心聚类问题推广到包含$z$个异常值（即在计算输入点到中心的最大距离时可以忽略$z$个输入点）的情况提供了已知$O(1)$-近似方法的加速，适用于高维欧几里得空间和汉明空间。

### [126] [Matrix Editing Meets Fair Clustering: Parameterized Algorithms and Complexity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03718)
*Robert Ganian,Hung P. Hoang,Simon Wietheger*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 该论文研究公平均值聚类问题，等价于通过最多修改k个值将彩色矩阵编辑为具有少量不同颜色平衡行的矩阵。虽然NP难，但作者排除了类似固定参数算法，并建立了完整的复杂度图谱，提出了三种规避下界的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究公平均值聚类问题的计算复杂性，该问题在公平设置下比传统聚类更具挑战性。虽然传统聚类问题已有固定参数算法，但公平设置下的复杂性尚不清楚，需要探索规避计算难度的途径。

Method: 1. 证明公平均值聚类问题即使在高度受限的情况下也不存在固定参数算法；2. 建立完整的复杂度图谱；3. 提出三种规避下界的方法：对问题实例施加额外约束、固定参数近似、使用针对树状矩阵的替代参数化。

Result: 1. 排除了公平均值聚类问题的固定参数算法；2. 建立了完整的复杂度图谱；3. 展示了三种规避下界的可行途径，为处理公平聚类问题提供了理论框架。

Conclusion: 公平均值聚类问题在计算上比传统聚类更具挑战性，但通过施加额外约束、使用近似算法或替代参数化方法，可以在某些情况下实现可处理性，为公平机器学习算法的设计提供了理论指导。

Abstract: We study the computational problem of computing a fair means clustering of discrete vectors, which admits an equivalent formulation as editing a colored matrix into one with few distinct color-balanced rows by changing at most $k$ values. While NP-hard in both the fairness-oblivious and the fair settings, the problem is well-known to admit a fixed-parameter algorithm in the former ``vanilla'' setting. As our first contribution, we exclude an analogous algorithm even for highly restricted fair means clustering instances. We then proceed to obtain a full complexity landscape of the problem, and establish tractability results which capture three means of circumventing our obtained lower bound: placing additional constraints on the problem instances, fixed-parameter approximation, or using an alternative parameterization targeting tree-like matrices.

中文标题: 矩阵编辑与公平聚类：参数化算法与复杂性

中文摘要: 我们研究计算离散向量的公平均值聚类的计算问题，该问题等价于通过最多改变k个值将彩色矩阵编辑为具有少量不同颜色平衡行的矩阵。虽然在公平无关和公平设置下都是NP难的，但该问题在传统的"普通"设置中已知具有固定参数算法。作为我们的第一个贡献，我们排除了即使是高度受限的公平均值聚类实例的类似算法。然后我们继续获得该问题的完整复杂度图谱，并建立了可处理性结果，这些结果捕捉了规避我们获得的下界的三种方法：对问题实例施加额外约束、固定参数近似、或使用针对树状矩阵的替代参数化。

</details>


### [127] [Robust Algorithms for Path and Cycle Problems in Geometric Intersection Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03843)
*Malory Marin,Jean-Florent Raymond,Rémi Watrigant*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种名为λ-linked partition的新工具，用于设计几何交图上的鲁棒亚指数算法，解决了哈密顿路径和哈密顿环问题的ETH紧算法，并扩展到了参数化长路径问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究几何交图上经典连通性问题的鲁棒亚指数算法设计，特别是解决de Berg等人提出的开放问题，完成从ETH紧精确算法角度对几何交图上这些问题的研究。

Method: 引入λ-linked partition作为核心工具，将顶点集划分为高度连通的组，可在多项式时间内计算且无需几何表示。结合几何交图的低树宽模式覆盖定理，设计算法框架。

Result: 获得了哈密顿路径和哈密顿环问题的首个鲁棒ETH紧算法，时间复杂度为2^{O(n^{1-1/d})}。设计了首个鲁棒亚指数参数化算法用于长路径问题，时间复杂度为2^{O(k^{1-1/d}log^2 k)} n^{O(1)}。

Conclusion: λ-linked partition是设计几何交图鲁棒算法的有效工具，解决了重要的开放问题，提出的低树宽模式覆盖定理具有独立研究价值，为几何交图算法设计提供了新框架。

Abstract: We study the design of robust subexponential algorithms for classical connectivity problems on intersection graphs of similarly sized fat objects in $\mathbb{R}^d$. In this setting, each vertex corresponds to a geometric object, and two vertices are adjacent if and only if their objects intersect. We introduce a new tool for designing such algorithms, which we call a $λ$-linked partition. This is a partition of the vertex set into groups of highly connected vertices. Crucially, such a partition can be computed in polynomial time and does not require access to the geometric representation of the graph. We apply this framework to problems related to paths and cycles in graphs. First, we obtain the first robust ETH-tight algorithms for Hamiltonian Path and Hamiltonian Cycle, running in time $2^{O(n^{1-1/d})}$ on intersection graphs of similarly sized fat objects in $\mathbb{R}^d$. This resolves an open problem of de Berg et al. [STOC 2018] and completes the study of these problems on geometric intersection graphs from the viewpoint of ETH-tight exact algorithms. We further extend our approach to the parameterized setting and design the first robust subexponential parameterized algorithm for Long Path in any fixed dimension $d$. More precisely, we obtain a randomized robust algorithm running in time $2^{O(k^{1-1/d}\log^2 k)}\, n^{O(1)}$ on intersection graphs of similarly sized fat objects in $\mathbb{R}^d$, where $k$ is the natural parameter. Besides $λ$-linked partitions, our algorithm also relies on a low-treewidth pattern covering theorem that we establish for geometric intersection graphs, which may be viewed as a refinement of a result of Marx-Pilipczuk [ESA 2017]. This structural result may be of independent interest.

中文标题: 几何交图中路径和循环问题的鲁棒算法

中文摘要: 我们研究了在ℝ^d中相似尺寸胖对象交图上经典连通性问题的鲁棒亚指数算法设计。在此设置中，每个顶点对应一个几何对象，当且仅当两个对象相交时，对应的顶点相邻。我们引入了一种设计此类算法的新工具，称为λ-linked partition。这是将顶点集划分为高度连通顶点组的一种划分。关键的是，这种划分可以在多项式时间内计算，并且不需要访问图的几何表示。我们将此框架应用于图中的路径和循环相关问题。首先，我们获得了哈密顿路径和哈密顿环问题的首个鲁棒ETH紧算法，在ℝ^d中相似尺寸胖对象交图上的运行时间为2^{O(n^{1-1/d})}。这解决了de Berg等人[STOC 2018]提出的开放问题，并从ETH紧精确算法的角度完成了这些在几何交图上的研究。我们进一步将方法扩展到参数化设置，并为任何固定维度d中的长路径问题设计了首个鲁棒亚指数参数化算法。更准确地说，我们获得了一个随机鲁棒算法，在ℝ^d中相似尺寸胖对象交图上的运行时间为2^{O(k^{1-1/d}log^2 k)} n^{O(1)}，其中k是自然参数。除了λ-linked partition，我们的算法还依赖于我们为几何交图建立的低树宽模式覆盖定理，这可以看作是Marx-Pilipczuk [ESA 2017]结果的改进。这一结构结果可能具有独立的研究价值。

</details>
